111@0~^~Peter DeMarco answers leadership questions from readers .~^~PERSON PERSON O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@1~^~Question .~^~O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@2~^~Our company performed very well this year .~^~O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@3~^~But now -- during the holidays !~^~O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@4~^~-- the CEO is telling us to cut costs by 5 percent in next year 's budget .~^~O O TITLE O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@5~^~How should I explain to my employees why we are cutting costs after a banner year of results ?~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@6~^~It does n't make sense to me , and I feel like Scrooge !~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@7~^~Answer .~^~O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@8~^~When budget cuts are directed , it 's natural to feel like Scrooge , the infamous miser from the Charles Dickens classic , A Christmas Carol .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O PERSON PERSON O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@9~^~Try to keep in mind the promise of the redeemed Scrooge : `` I will honor Christmas in my heart , and try to keep it all the year .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@10~^~I will live in the Past , the Present , and the Future .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@11~^~The Spirits of all Three shall strive within me .~^~O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@12~^~I will not shut out the lessons that they teach ! ''~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@14~^~Most CEOs learn from the past and celebrate the wins in the present .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@15~^~But the best CEOs make decisions and set priorities based on what they believe will happen in the future .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@16~^~As a leader it 's your duty to make sense of company mandates for your employees .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@17~^~Delivering difficult messages about cost cutting during the Christmas season is not easy .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@18~^~So before you communicate to your team about the cuts , take the time to understand why they are being directed , and what should be said .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@19~^~Assuming your CEO is competent -LRB- and not an unredeemed Scrooge -RRB- , several reasons would justify the cost-cutting : Markets : The market may be declining in size .~^~O O TITLE O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@20~^~While employees tend to measure their performance against the prior year , top CEOs measure performance against the market potential in the future and the capacity of their organization to respond to it .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@21~^~Depending on the investment time horizon , excess capacity must either be absorbed through growth or cut to avoid lower profits or losses .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@22~^~For example , after several years of growth , analysts expect the mortgage market to decline next year due to a combination of factors , such as rising interest rates and flat wage growth. , Expenses : Perhaps free cash is being spent , rather than invested .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@23~^~When businesses are making money , managers have a tendency to spend the profits on non-value added projects or activities that do not provide a return above the risk level of the business. , Value : Valuation may be an issue .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@24~^~The board of directors may be putting the business up for sale at its peak value .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@25~^~To maximize value further , every dollar saved generates a multiplier on the value of the business. , Investments : There may be a better way to use or invest the company 's profits .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@26~^~Possibly your business is treated as a cash cow and is being milked for all of its profits to be deployed elsewhere .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@28~^~These are all generally good reasons for cutting costs .~^~O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@29~^~There are also bad reasons for cutting costs .~^~O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@30~^~Your CEO may have failed to define a clear and compelling direction for the organization 's future to shareholders .~^~ORGANIZATION TITLE O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@31~^~In this situation , a competent board of directors identifies the lack of vibrant leadership as a sign of coasting on the past and status-quo thinking .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@32~^~Thus , a short-term focus on cutting costs is invoked to shake things up , reveal hidden waste and stay competitive .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@33~^~Or your CEO may be risk averse , unable to see future opportunities beyond the success of the current year .~^~O O TITLE O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@34~^~Cost cutting sometimes comes out of a miserly view that sees the present success as unlikely to continue .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@35~^~Unfortunately , cutting costs often includes reducing staff .~^~O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@36~^~Nobody likes doing a layoff before Christmas .~^~O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@37~^~It leaves employees and managers with survivor 's guilt during a time that is supposed to be filled with joy , especially for children .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@38~^~But the alternative of waiting to communicate these decisions -LRB- which are beyond your control -RRB- until after the holidays often makes things worse for the affected employees and their families .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@39~^~They may end up saddled with more debt and expenses than they might have incurred had they known sooner .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@40~^~While time is of the essence , employ a constructive path of inquiry to discover the reasons behind your CEO 's cost-cutting mandate .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O TITLE O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@41~^~Ask questions .~^~O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@42~^~Your human resources department ought to be able to help too .~^~ORGANIZATION O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@43~^~Then , with the information you obtain , seek out a leader you trust to help formulate good answers .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@44~^~Once you 've made sense of things for yourself , you 'll be able to communicate more effectively with your employees .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@45~^~They wo n't expect you to know everything , but they will expect you to share what information is available to you .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@46~^~It 's not a pleasant task , but they 'll appreciate your efforts to explain why the cost cutting is occurring and how it will affect them , even during the holidays .~^~O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
111@47~^~Peter DeMarco is founder and president of Priority Thinking , an executive coaching , organizational consulting , strategy advisement , and ethics education company .~^~PERSON PERSON O TITLE O TITLE O ORGANIZATION ORGANIZATION O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O O~^~n/a~^~N/A
